883                        "        function foo() {\n" + 
884                        "                var i = 0;\n" + 
885                        "                System.out.println(\n" + 
886                        "                        \" \" + (i + 1)); \n" + 
887                        "}\n";
888 
889        String completeBehind = "i + 1";
890        String expectedCompletionNodeToString = NONE;
891        String completionIdentifier = "";
892        String expectedUnitDisplayString = null;
893        String expectedReplacedSource = NONE;
894        String testName = "<complete on digit into method call argument>";
895

897

899                checkMethodParse(

905                        expectedReplacedSource,

908        } catch(InvalidCursorLocation e){

910        }
911}
